<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><span style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><b>Item&#160;8.01</b></span> <span style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><b>Other Events.</b></span></p>


<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Zion
Oil and Gas, Inc., a Delaware corporation, which has an active petroleum exploration license onshore Israel on their 99,000-acre Megiddo-Jezreel
license area<span style="background-color: white">&#160;announces that it </span>has completed the drilling of their Megiddo-Jezreel
#2 (MJ02) well to a total depth of 5,531 meters (18,141 feet) with a six-inch (6&#8221;) open hole at that depth. The primary zone of
interest contains encouraging shows of hydrocarbons.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">A
full set of detailed and comprehensive tests including neutron-density, sonic, gamma, and resistivity logs, paired with well testing,
will commence during the coming weeks. Based on these logs and analysis, additional zones of interest may be identified and tested. All
testing equipment and personnel are in Israel, and Zion is assembling the required equipment at the well site for the comprehensive testing.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#160;</span></p>



<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><b>Item&#160;9.01
&#160;Financial Statements and Exhibits.</b></span></p>


<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">(d)
Exhibits</span></p>

<DESCRIPTION>PRESS RELEASE DATED NOVEMBER 23, 2021
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="text-align: right; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Zion Oil &amp; Gas Completes Drilling Phase of the Megiddo-Jezreel
#2 (MJ-02) Well in Israel</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Zion moves forward with testing based on encouraging shows of hydrocarbons.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">DALLAS, Texas, and CAESAREA,
Israel, November 23, 2021 /PRNewswire/&nbsp;</FONT>Zion Oil &amp; Gas, Inc. <FONT STYLE="background-color: white">(OTCQX: ZNOG) announces
the completion of the drilling phase for their Megiddo-Jezreel #2 (MJ-02) well.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&ldquo;We are thankful for the successful completion of our drilling
phase,&rdquo; expressed Zion Oil &amp; Gas CEO, Robert Dunn. &ldquo;We are eager to move forward with testing immediately based on encouraging
hydrocarbon shows.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: center; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><IMG SRC="ex99-1_001.jpg" ALT="">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: center; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">Zion Drilling Rig in Israel.
Photo taken on November 22, 2021.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Zion has completed the drilling of the MJ02 well to a total depth of
5,531 meters (18,141 feet) with a six-inch (6&rdquo;) open hole at that depth.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">The primary zone of interest contains encouraging shows of hydrocarbons.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">A full set of detailed and comprehensive tests including neutron-density,
sonic, gamma, and resistivity logs, paired with well testing, will commence during the coming weeks. Based on these logs and analysis,
additional zones of interest may be identified and tested.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">All testing equipment and personnel are in Israel, and Zion is assembling
the required equipment at the well site for the comprehensive testing.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">Zion Oil &amp; Gas, a public
company, traded on OTCQX Best Market, explores for oil and gas onshore in Israel on their 99,000-acre Megiddo-Jezreel license area. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><I>&ldquo;The Lord Himself goes before you and
will be with you; He will never leave you nor forsake you.<BR>
 Do not be afraid; do not be discouraged.&rdquo; </I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><I>Deuteronomy 31:8</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><I>&ldquo;Sing to the Lord, for he has done glorious
things; let this be known to all the world. Shout aloud<BR>
 and sing for joy, people of Zion, for great is the Holy One of Israel among you.&rdquo;
</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><I>Isaiah 12:5-6</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">FORWARD-LOOKING STATEMENTS: Statements
in this communication that are not historical fact, including, but not limited to, statements regarding Zion&rsquo;s operations and the
results therefrom, including testing and completion; Zion's ability to discover and produce oil in commercial quantities; Zion&rsquo;s
ability to continue as a going concern; operational risks in ongoing exploration efforts; the timing and completion of the processing,
interpretation of the results and plans contingent thereon of the 3-D seismic survey; regulatory approvals needed for the rig&rsquo;s
operation; the effect, if any, of the coronavirus pandemic on the timing of the operation of the well, and liquidity for shareholders
on OTCQX are forward-looking statements as defined in the &ldquo;Safe Harbor&rdquo; provisions of the Private Securities Litigation Reform
Act of 1995. These forward-looking statements are based on assumptions that are subject to significant known and unknown risks, uncertainties,
and other unpredictable factors, many of which are described in Zion&rsquo;s periodic reports filed with the SEC and are beyond Zion&rsquo;s
control. These risks could cause Zion&rsquo;s actual performance to differ materially from the results predicted by these forward-looking
statements. These risks and uncertainties include, but are not limited to, those described in Item 1A in Zion&rsquo;s Annual Report on
Form 10-K, which is expressly incorporated herein by reference, and other factors as may periodically be described in Zion&rsquo;s filings
with the SEC. Zion can give no assurance that the expectations reflected in these statements will prove to be correct and assumes no responsibility
to update these statements.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">Contact Info:</FONT></P>
